2023 Panini Select Football Checklist, Team Set Lists and Details

2023 Football Cards, Checklists, Checklists-New, New
By Ryan Cracknell - September 3, 2024
September 3, 2024
4
When you click on links to various merchants on this site, like eBay, and make a purchase, this can result in this site earning a commission.
Share:

Jump to the 2023 Panini Select Football checklist and team set lists.

The 2023 Panini Select Football checklist is big and colorful. Chrome is the centerpiece once again, opening things up for all sorts of parallels. Things grow exponentially when the various levels of the base set are taken into account. It’s not just base cards and parallels, though. Autographs, memorabilia cards and a generous assortment of inserts are also part of the wide-reaching release.

As far as hobby box hits go, there are two autographs and one memorabilia card. Parallels are also plentiful, combining to fall 15 per box.

2023 Panini Select Football Checklist Overview

The full Select base set has 500 cards, matching 2022. It’s not quite so straightforward, though. It has five different sections, each with varying levels of rarity and mix of parallels. With some players appearing multiple times, it makes for a lot of cards to chase.

Among Select’s autograph content are some that also include memorabilia. Prime Selections and Rookie Jumbo Swatches are two such sets, both with oversized pieces of gear.

Taking from the base set’s vibe, standard inserts also take different levels of rarity. For those looking for the toughest sets, Color Wheel and new-to-football Starcade are among them. There’s also Select Anniversary.

One thing that Select Football continues to have that the brand doesn’t use in other sports is XRC Redemptions. These are good for players from the 2023 NFL Draft.

2023 Panini Select Football cards at a glance:

Cards per pack: Hobby – 5
Packs per box: Hobby – 12
Boxes per case: Hobby – 12
Set size: 500 cards
Release date: August 30, 2024

Shop for 2023 Panini Select Football boxes on eBay:

  • Hobby Boxes
  • 1st Off the Line Boxes
  • Mega Boxes
  • Blaster Boxes
  • Hanger Boxes

What to expect in a hobby box:

  • Autographs – 2
  • Memorabilia Cards – 1
  • Prizms Parallels – 15

2023 Panini Select Football Checklist

You can also download a customizable spreadsheet copy of the checklist:

  • 2023 Panini Select Football Checklist – XLSX File

Please note that print runs for cards without serial numbers have not been announced.

Ryan Cracknell

A collector for much of his life, Ryan focuses primarily on building sets, Montreal Expos and other interesting cards. He's also got one of the most comprehensive collections of John Jaha cards in existence (not that there are a lot of them).
